<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gepeperd.html>gepeperd</a> (106314)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gepeperd.html>gepeperd</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gepeperd.html>gepeperder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gepeperdst</b>)

<ol><li>peppered, seasoned with pepper(s)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> spicy, strongly flavored</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> extreme, strong, <a href = vnd.unilang:etcetera.html>etcetera</a></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:geranium.html>geranium</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γέρανος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">géranos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***gerbil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerbil.html>gerbil</a> (75758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">gerbille</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gerbo</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">جَرْبُوع</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jarbūʿ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">يَرْبُوع</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yarbūʿ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jerboa</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerbil.html>gerbil</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gerbils</b>)
</p>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/gerbil" class="extiw" title="w:gerbil"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerbil.html>gerbil</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/gerbil" class="extiw" title="w:gerbil">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<ol><li>One of several species of small, <a href = vnd.unilang:jumping.html>jumping</a>, murine rodents, of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gerbillus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gerbillus"><i>Gerbillus</i></a></span> and certain other genera in subfamily Gerbillinae, with leaping powers resembling the jerboa, native to Africa, India, and Southern Europe.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerbil.html>gerbil</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">gerbils</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gerbilling</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gerbiling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gerbilled</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gerbiled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To rotate inside a monowheel or similar apparatus due to sudden acceleration or braking.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To insert a small animal into one's <a href = vnd.unilang:rectum.html>rectum</a> (a sexual practice in urban myth).</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:zoogdieren.html>zoogdieren</a>)</span> <i>Gerbillinae</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ondersoort.html>ondersoort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:familie.html>familie</a> <i>Muridae</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarnaast.html>daarnaast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muizen.html>muizen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ratten.html>ratten</a>, stekelmuizen <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwanten.html>verwanten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omvat.html>omvat</a></li></ol>

***gerecht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a> (5968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gerichte</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechte.html>gerechte</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">court of law</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gerihte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*garihtiją</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">something prepared or arranged</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gerihte</i>. The sense "dish" developed independently already in Old Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gerihte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">meal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechten.html>gerechten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerechtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> justice; the judiciary</li>
<li>court of law</li>
<li>a meal, or a dish served alone or part of a meal as a course</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:justitie.html>justitie</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">rechtscollege</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schotel.html>schotel</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gherecht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gereht</i> (in <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gerehto</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*garehtaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌲𐌰𐍂𐌰𐌹𐌷𐍄𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">garaihts</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">geriht</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerechter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gerechtst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>just, fair, deserved</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Onderwijsinspectie <a href = vnd.unilang:hoeft.html>hoeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vernietigend.html>vernietigend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rapport.html>rapport</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Cornelius Haga <a href = vnd.unilang:lyceum.html>Lyceum</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trekken.html>trekken</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechtshof.html>gerechtshof</a></b> in Den <a href = vnd.unilang:haag.html>Haag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:hoger.html>hoger</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitspreken.html>uitspreken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> rechtmatigheid <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> document.</i><sup id="cite_ref-Gerechtshof_brandt_vingers_niet_aan_inspectierapport_over_Haga_Lyceum_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Gerechtshof_brandt_vingers_niet_aan_inspectierapport_over_Haga_Lyceum-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gereed.html>gereed</a> (2210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gereet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*girēde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*garaidijaz</i>, prefixed form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raidijaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raidaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gereed.html>gereed</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gereed.html>gereed</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gereed.html>gereed</a></b>)

<ol><li>ready, prepared</li>
<li>done, finished, completed</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">reasonable</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">serious</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rechter.html>rechter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geeft.html>geeft</a> (in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geheim.html>geheim</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toestemming.html>toestemming</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afluisteren.html>afluisteren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gerede.html>gerede</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdenkingen.html>verdenkingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaan.html>bestaan</a>.</i> ("<a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>Met</a> 'Obama-gate' <a href = vnd.unilang:onthutst.html>onthutst</a> Trump <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfs.html>zelfs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:republikeinen.html>Republikeinen</a>", in the newspaper <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a>, 6 March 2017)
<dl><dd>In case of <b>reasonable</b> suspicions, a judge will give (in secret) his permission for a wiretap.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:geren.html>geren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">geron</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*gerēn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gerōną</i>, related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gernaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to eager, willing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
